<a name="s183782EC2667435A57D353EEA6001BFF"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:14pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:14pt;font-weight:bold;">Lawson Products Reports Second Quarter 2015 Results</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">$2.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;improvement in operating income</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">$0.33 EPS on net sales of $70.7 million</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">CHICAGO, </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">July&#160;23, 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;- Lawson Products, Inc. (NASDAQ:LAWS) (</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">&#8220;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Lawson</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">&#8221;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;or the "Company")</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, a distributor of products and services to the MRO marketplace, today announced results for the second quarter ended </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">. The Company generated $3.2 million of operating income on net sales of $70.7 million.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">"We delivered improved operating results,&#8221; said Michael DeCata, president and chief executive officer. &#8220;Sales continued to be impacted by the weaker Canadian dollar and reduced demand in the energy sector which has contributed to a broader based slow-down across the MRO marketplace.  Those factors aside, we realized solid growth within many of our strategic customer relationships while at the same time achieved continued operating metric improvements.  Our gross margins, which expanded to 61.9% during the quarter, combined with our effective cost control efforts and increased productivity, yielded a significant improvement in our operating income. These improvements further demonstrate that previous changes to our infrastructure are delivering benefits.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">"Our continued improvement in operating results re-confirms that customers value our business model. We ended the quarter with 920 sales representatives.  We remain committed to expanding our sales force and refining processes to improve their early success with us,&#8221; continued Mr. DeCata.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;text-decoration:underline;">Financial Highlights</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8226;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"></font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Net sales declined to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$70.7 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the second quarter of 2015, compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$72.1 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the second quarter a year ago.</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Gross margins continued to increase to 61.9% for the quarter compared to 60.8% a year ago. This improvement continues a trend exceeding 61% of net sales for the third straight quarter.</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;background-color:#ffffff;">&#8226;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"></font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">GAAP operating income was $3.2 million for the quarter, up $2.0 million from $1.2 million a year ago. Non-GAAP adjusted operating income improved </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$2.2 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$4.3 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the second quarter of 2015 compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$2.1 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the second quarter of 2014 (See reconciliation in Table 1).</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Net income improved to $2.9 million ($0.33 EPS per diluted share) compared to $0.8 million ($0.09 EPS per diluted share) a year ago.</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Cash flow from operations was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$4.2 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the second quarter. Lawson ended the quarter with no debt outstanding and </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$5.4 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of available cash on hand.</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;text-decoration:underline;">Second Quarter Results</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Net sales for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second quarter of 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;decreased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">1.9%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$70.7 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;from </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$72.1 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second quarter of 2014</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;impacted by the decrease in the Canadian exchange rate, weak demand from customers associated with the oil and gas industry and a general slow-down in the MRO marketplace. Demand during the quarter from our direct oil and gas customers declined </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$1.4 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;from a year ago quarter; however, has leveled-out from the first quarter. Excluding this decline and the Canadian exchange rate impact of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$0.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, net sales increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">1.4%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;from the prior year quarter (See reconciliation in Table 2). This increase was driven primarily by our Kent Automotive Division and growing current strategic account relationships. </font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s183782EC2667435A57D353EEA6001BFF"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Overall, average daily sales decreased to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$1.105 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second quarter of 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$1.126 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the prior year quarter.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Gross profit for the period improved to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">61.9%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">60.8%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the second quarter of 2014 and </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">61.3%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the first quarter. This increase was due primarily to our continuing efforts to improve distribution efficiencies and lower purchasing costs.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Selling expenses decreased to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$21.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second quarter of 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;from </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$23.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the prior year quarter and as a percent of sales, decreased to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">31.0%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">31.8%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">. The $1.1 million decrease was primarily driven by reduced performance based compensation, lower commissions on lower net sales and continued cost control efforts, offset partially by higher fixed compensation of newly hired sales representatives. General and administrative expenses decreased to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$18.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second quarter of 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;from </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$19.5 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the prior year quarter due primarily to lower performance based compensation and severance expense, and continued cost control measures. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">GAAP operating income improved to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$3.2 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;from </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$1.2 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;a year ago. Excluding certain non-operational and non-recurring items, adjusted non-GAAP operating income was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$4.3 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the second quarter of 2015 compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$2.1 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;a year ago (See reconciliation in Table 1). On a year-to-date basis, adjusted non-GAAP operating income improved by </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$3.1 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;over a year ago. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;text-indent:12px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Net income for the second quarter of 2015 was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$2.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$0.33</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$0.8 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$0.09</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share, for the same period a year ago.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">The Company generated $4.2 million of cash flows from operations in the quarter and ended the quarter with $5.4 million of available cash and no debt.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">"In summary, I am pleased with our performance this quarter. We will continue to refine our processes, add sales people in targeted markets and utilize our strong financial position to pursue growth opportunities," concluded Mr. DeCata.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;text-decoration:underline;">Conference Call</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Lawson Products, Inc., will conduct a conference call with investors to discuss second quarter 2015 results at 9:00 a.m. EDT on </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">July&#160;23, 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">. Lawson Products serves the industrial, commercial, institutional and government maintenance, repair and operations (MRO) market. The Company ships products to customers in all 50 states, Puerto Rico, Canada, Mexico and the Caribbean from five strategically located distribution centers in North America. Under its Kent Automotive brand, the Company supplies products to collision and mechanical repair shops as well as automotive OEMs. For additional information, please visit </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;text-decoration:underline;">www.lawsonproducts.com</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">This Release contains certain forward-looking statements within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995 that involve risks and uncertainties.
